································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································································ **True Parents' Day and Our Family**
[Prayer]
Beloved Father! Today is March 28, 1979, the first day of the third lunar month. This day is also a day of memories when True Parents' Day was proclaimed 19 years ago. In a complex environment, where no one acknowledges it, in an environment where only You acknowledge it, we thank You once again for this day, which became the day to proclaim a new start on this earth with the name of True Parents. I recall that day far away in Korea, which heralded a historical new beginning for the resolution of Your wishes and desires, blocking the historical sorrows that were many. 

We have crossed many tedious stages to reach this 20th anniversary. From individuals to families, tribes, nations, and the world, how much have You, Father, grieved, and how much has humanity groaned in misery? We know that once we betray Your will, we cannot pass over the history of indemnity without paying the price before the whole crowd without forgiveness.

Our Ideal World
The word "we" refers to the plural. Therefore, this "we" includes not only the audience here but also the Unification Church and all of humanity. When viewed this way, the phrase "humanity and the ideal world" also applies.

What is the ideal world? In our Unification Church, we say, "The ideal world is the earthly paradise." It has achieved heaven. This year's slogan is also expressed in terms of family church and heaven, but the earthly paradise and the ideal world converge to one purpose, the same purpose.

Every human being hopes for the arrival of the ideal world.
Many people living on this earth vaguely hope for an ideal world to come. What exactly is that ideal world? "It is a place of freedom and peace. Therefore, it is a place where humanity lives as one." This is quite vague. However, in our Unification Church, it is not vague at all. We present specific content. We say it is a world of peace, freedom, and unification, but the question is, what comes first and what comes last? "The world of unification comes first." Some people say freedom, and some say peace. They exchange ideas, asking, "Can there be unification without peace?" They also say, "There can be no unification without freedom, and there can be no peace without freedom." All of that is good. 

However, what our Unification Church presents is that while these elements are important, the very first thing must be love. We assert that love is the central noun. Freedom centered on love is connected. It is welcomed anywhere. Furthermore, peace centered on love is welcomed wherever it goes. Unification centered on love can also be welcomed at any time. Without that, order cannot be established. The concept of freedom differs between the democratic world and the communist world. Their views of peace are also different. Their views of unification are different as well. However, no matter how different the content may be, if love is connected to it, it can harmonize and manifest in one form, which is beyond question. Why is that? What the people of the communist world demand is love, and what the people of the democratic world demand is also love. Essentially, they cannot be different. What kind of love is that? It is a love that can connect cause and effect. This means that it has not changed from the past to the present and will not change forever.

The most problematic issue in the free world today is the order of love. What is the most difficult problem in the free world? It is the issue of the order of love. Love is love, but what kind of love is it? It is the love between a man and a woman. Such love lacks historical process, future perspective, and direction. It is love that is self-indulgent. (Laughter) Such love cannot be the source of freedom, the source of unification, or the source of peace. 

People who love each other today may be happy but will separate tomorrow; what kind of peace is there in that, what kind of unification is there, what kind of freedom is there? Is there freedom there? Is there happiness there? Is there peace there? Is there unification there? Everything is the opposite, everything. Such love leads to destruction. It is a motive for destruction and an unacceptable content. That love is a strategic weapon that Satan uses to destroy humanity and to destroy the ideals of humanity, and you must understand that. It takes away true peace from us, takes away true freedom from us, and takes away true unification from us; we must recognize that it is a strategic method of the enemy.

However, if there is Satan, there is also God. What about God? It is the opposite. It is the absolute opposite. When viewed from the perspective of love with tradition, a love that can connect cause and effect is evil, an enemy, and an unacceptable sin. It is an enemy before God and an unacceptable sin. What kind of sin is it? It is the most terrible sin. It is the enemy that God hates the most. If that path is not corrected, God treats it as an enemy and a sin, and thus it leads to destruction. Destruction is the principle.

Some of you may have visited Pompeii in Italy, but that city was destroyed due to a society of disordered love. Sodom and Gomorrah were destroyed for the same reason. You must understand that Rome also fell for this reason. Based on this official historical perspective, if America does not correct such love and does not repent, it will fall. It will surely fall. If such an order of love does not establish itself in America, there is no freedom. There is no peace, nor is there any possibility of unification. We must recognize the fact that chaos, ruin, and darkness are looming. Is that right? "Yes." If you, the members of the Unification Church sitting here, cannot determine your path from this perspective and cannot specify your position, you will fall.

Our Unification Church longs for the ideal world more than anyone else, and because we are at the forefront of completing the heavenly kingdom on earth, we need more peace, more freedom, and more unification. Therefore, what is the important issue we must establish here? It is that before we can find ourselves aligned with eternal love as a center, we can conclude that everything is in vain. That is why we seek this path.

True love is desired by everyone. True love is the love that God would like if He exists. Also, if there have been saints and sages throughout history who have desired the happiness of humanity and envisioned the ideals of humanity, it is the love they desire and want. And it is the love that all those who walk the true path of humanity in this world and who wish to become the center of this world through their faith want and desire.

What we must leave for our true descendants is not money, nor the doomed free world, nor the peace they advocate, nor the unification world they advocate. It is not knowledge, nor power, nor anything else. It is not about looking good either. What the descendants truly want is true love. They say, "Please grant me true love!" 

If that love exists, there is freedom, ideals, and everything. Therefore, our Unification Church has determined that this is certain. Also, God sees it that way, all the saints and sages see it that way, the idealists of humanity today see it that way, and it is certain that future descendants will wish for it that way. That is why we must seek the path centered on love. That is what God desires, what the saints and sages desire, what the idealists of this age desire, and what the true descendants want.

On the day we hold onto that love and carry it to completion, God will follow, the saints and sages will follow, countless religious people will follow, and countless descendants will follow. That is the conclusion. Do you think so? "Yes." That is the most important thing. Is there anyone who disagrees with this? "No." Anyone who disagrees should have their head examined. Have you finished the maintenance? 「Yes」 Will you be able to go straight without veering off? 
「Yes」 Do you think there will be no accidents where you might say, 'Oh no, this is a big problem' if something breaks down while you're going? 「Yes」 What if someone pulls you from behind? Will you pull them along, or will you be pulled? 「I will pull them along」 Really? 「Yes」 What does 'yes' mean? I will try to hit you once. You guys, is that really true? Then you can fly anywhere with a swoosh, right?
 When it comes to flying… if it's an airplane, there is a limit to the number of people it can carry, 
a limit. If it has 360 seats, then there are 360 seats. You have to fill that capacity to fly. That is ideal. In there, your husbands will be included, your wives will be included, your sons and daughters will be included, and all your relatives will be included. Everyone, what kind of church should the home church be next? 「……」 Then should only white people board? Should black people stop? 「No」 Then what kind of people should board? 「People of all colors」 
All colors, all colors must board. Then it will go through the country and through the world….
 How far do we need to go? We must go to the point where we can say, 'I will embrace the world with God's love.' In other words, the influence of my love, the power of my love, operates through a global foundation all the way to the heavenly kingdom and the infinite spiritual world. We must think that it can reach that far. This airplane flies on the earth, but from here on, what is it? It’s a satellite flying. It flies to the heavenly kingdom. (Pointing to what he wrote on the board, smiling)
 When you launch a rocket, the moon is to the east, but the rocket is launched to the west. What this means is that people who do not know the principle are like those who are called crazy about the principle. (Laughs)
 However, the compass of the rocket, the compass of the airplane, and the compass of the ship are all the same. You need to know that. The only difference is whether it is flat or vertical. So if you feel that love, you will definitely become a rocket and fly away.
 Following that line, if it does not get destroyed, God will go and boom…. (Laughs) If that happens, God can finally explode with true love, and if God is happy, the whole world can dance at once, and it becomes a world of peace.
 If God dances, will the world dance along or not? Think about it. 「We will dance together」 If the mother and father are dancing, then the sons and daughters will all dance too, right? If God becomes intoxicated with love and dances, then this world will melt away. What if God runs around and steps on your heads? Would you say, 'Please step on me!' or would you say, 'Phew'? 
156  
What do you think? 「I will ask to be stepped on」 Will that become one or not? Think about it. 「It will become one」 
Live a life of sacrifice and service centered on love
 Now, even if the Buddhas fight among themselves, when a woman asks, 'Did you love me with your true love?' and the man replies, 'Well! I said I loved you, but I don't know. Is that a failure?' then the woman says, 'Okay. Just stay still!' and then it becomes 'Okay'. This is how it goes. (Laughs) No matter how big and dignified the husband is, when asked if he has shown true love, if he says he hasn't, then even if he says 'stay still!'…. No matter how good he is at fighting, when centered on love, if he says 'stay still', it will be 'yes', not 'what's that?' 
Also, even if the husband wears a tie and has a good figure, when asked, 'In loving, do you love our children and our family more than me?' if he says 'I can't', then if she says 'then you have to listen to me', he will say 'yes', not 'no'. Now, how simple is this? When asking the president of the country, 'Did you love the people more than your parents, more than anyone else?' if he says he didn't…. This principle is an important issue.
 After having such a direction and position, how should we live? We must live a life of sacrifice and service centered on love. What is the way of life? It is the life of sacrifice and service. That is how parents live, and that is how God lives. Teachers should also do the same, and any leaders of organizations, the president of a country, and God Himself must follow this. That is the way of life, the way of life.
 If this happens, the environment of heaven will surely unfold. This is our strategy to quickly bind all stories in the human world with love and create one heaven. Now, do you understand? 「Yes」
 We must have a purpose. That purpose is the ideal world, and the direction is the direction of love, and then what is the way of life? 「Sacrifice and service」 Then you must always know how to discern your position. The closer that position gets, the heavier the burden becomes. It does not get lighter; it gets heavier. Reflections on a lifetime
Today is June 1st, June 1st. Therefore, all of nature is now entering into summer, heading towards the full-fledged summer, entering a lush season.

Our internal and external efforts are combined.
Everyone, among the trees at the Belvedere training center, there is a big zelkova tree, and when we see that tree, we tend to think, 'Ah! That is a good tree,' and pass by simply. Wherever you go, when you go to a garden, you always think about the best trees, the best flowers, the best-looking trees, the biggest trees. However, it is extremely difficult to have that beautiful form that can be called 'beautiful.'

To achieve that beauty... You must think that the elements that can bring forth that beauty are necessarily involved behind it. Whether it is artificial or natural, it is more difficult to be natural than to be artificial. And the seed of that one tree is extremely small, but to grow that seed into that big tree, you must understand that many elements around it are sacrificed for that tree to grow. 

Before the tree boasts, 'Ah, I am so big and beautiful! I am the best!' it will not think, 'I did not become this way on my own; all the surrounding things came together for me to become this way.' If the tree were to think like that, it would say, 'Ah, I have grown,' but before boasting, it would say, 'I must respect all the elements that have been sacrificed and absorbed for me.'

Then, if the soil around that tree thinks, 'This guy knows that,' or if all the surrounding elements have sacrificed themselves, they might think, 'This guy is good.' The grass under its shade might think, 'I dislike the shade, but since you are like that, I am okay with it.' (laughter)

When thinking about this, when asked, 'Why have you grown so big?' it is not about boasting for itself, but rather about the harmony of all the elements behind it, and the inner and outer efforts that can create such a form. 

And no matter how much the tree boasts, what will happen when the sunlight disappears? Will the feeling of boasting come first, or the worry about the absence of sunlight? What is it? Will boasting come first, or worry? "Worry." Also, if you think, 'Oh, the air is gone. (laughter) Then, what if the water is gone? 'Hey, you have no water, what will you do?' It’s the same.

You must not think, "I must snatch that man." Therefore, when looking at a man, you see through the glasses of the husband. Also, when looking at a woman, you must see through the glasses of the wife. Do you understand what that means?

When that happens, one family becomes an extended world. For you, what determines ownership or value? It is determined by how much you extend this from here. If this happens, it will automatically connect. (Pointing to what he wrote) True horizontal love automatically generates true vertical love, and true vertical love automatically generates true horizontal love. For example, where there is perfect negative electricity, there will naturally be perfect positive electricity. Those who think this way, no matter how ugly their face is, everyone will like them. Do you understand what I’m saying? "Yes." 

If you were born white, what did you do to black people? What did you do to yellow people? That is the problem. Do you understand what I’m saying? "Yes." 

Can Reverend Moon be welcomed only in white society? "No." Can he be welcomed only in Asia? "No." Only in the black world? "No." So what kind of principle must it be? It must be a principle of love. Do you understand? "Yes." And you, up until now in the Unification Church, what has the Unification Church given you? "It has given us love." So the teacher is trying to give you this, but do you have this love? "Yes." Are you in the process of receiving it, or have you received it? "Both." Which one is ahead, which one? There will be three types of people: those who are trying to receive, those who are receiving, and those who are just watching.

Now, if someone says, "I have been in the Unification Church for 10 years, 20 years," and sits there chattering, "I have tried everything you do," what category does that person belong to? They only know how to eat, and they want to do all the good things themselves and make others do the bad things. Also, some long-time members say, "The church should help me; I have helped the church until now." They are saying that. They should forget about helping the church. Helping the church is a stage of restoration. Even if they still have the intention to help the country and the world, they should not just cling to the church. They must lead the church.

Is the Unification Church leading Reverend Moon, or is Reverend Moon leading the Unification Church? "The teacher is leading." The same goes for Unification Church members. Are they leading the Unification Church, or is the Unification Church leading the Unification Church members? "Unification Church members are leading the Unification Church." They must know the path that the church should take and run ahead to open the way.

You all gathered here this morning because the Unification Church called you, and you were drawn to the Unification Church. Did you gather to lead the Unification Church? "We gathered to lead." Really? "Yes." You gather a lot when the teacher is present, but when the teacher is not present, you should gather even more. You all should come more and take the place of the teacher. (Applause) You should do as much as Reverend Moon does.

Look, your eternal ownership is determined in this world of love, and authority is determined here. What you always do is this. Now, when school-going children ask their parents for money, it’s good, but when they meet them, they say, "Hey, study, study!" and when they come back from school, they say, "Oh, study!" and they dislike it. (Laughter) It’s the same. When you say, "Mr. Park, do this, do that," they want to do it even less. Is that true? "No." 

If I do that, does food come out, does money come out? "No." I am doing that while spending money. The more you move, the more it costs, right? Do you understand? Why? Because to make excellent people in society, and to make excellent people in the future in that country, it cannot be otherwise. When God quietly looks at the history of the world centered on this principle, how much will He praise Reverend Moon, and how much will He hold on to him? (Applause)

No matter how much you push and do whatever, you must create a foundation that can be tangled up centered on love. Everyone must be able to marry on the world stage. Who has done that until now? "No one." Now, this time, you all had engagement blessings, but will that be the end of it? Will you expand it more dimensionally? "We will expand it dimensionally." When Africa looks at it, they will say, "That Reverend Moon did something wrong," and when Asia looks at it, they will say, "Ah, that’s why he did something wrong," and will America itself say, "That was wrong"? If they cannot do it themselves, they should try it once and do more than that and then evaluate me; if they don’t do it and just make a fuss, then who will survive, and who will win? Who? "Us." It’s not us; it’s the country, it’s me. 

The completion of the vertical and horizontal realms is a form that can align the east, west, south, north, up, down, left, and right of the universe. 

What is today’s sermon title? "What do I have?" What do you have?
Do you have it? The ideal of the son-in-law. What do you have? I have the ideal of the son-in-law. Without this, the entire world will break apart. The universe will break apart. I am going out to establish this foundation. For this purpose, I need a wife and children. The ideal of the son-in-law is a form that can align the entire universe in all directions, up and down, left and right.

Now, can this be exchanged with America? "No." It cannot be exchanged even for the universe. You must understand that it cannot be exchanged even for God and the True Parents. This love is that great. Do you want to have it just once? "Yes." How much have I wanted it to be something I can sing about, something valuable, something radiant, something hopeful? This is the point where the misaligned gears of the universe have been adjusted perfectly through the ideal of the son-in-law.

Everyone, when you go to the river, there are smooth stones. How long have they rolled? How many times have they bumped and been pushed? Similarly, people change because of such experiences. Both the talented and the untalented get polished. At that time, you must say, "No matter what, I will not break. I will only become stronger and rounder." Are you confident about that? "Yes." Are those who receive the engagement blessing all confident about that? "Yes."

At first, it's like, "Oh, this is nice," but after some time, they think, "What’s nice about it? Oh, it’s ugly," and they start comparing with their old lovers and brothers. "I don’t do that." That’s good. (Laughter) But while they doubt each other, in the end, they even doubt the teacher. "Why did I have to be with someone like this?" Right? "No." How long, for how many days is it "No"? For how many years? "Forever." Why? Why? Why is that? It is because we have this theoretical basis. As a representative of America, as a representative of the world, I am needed. The two of us standing there is the original purpose. It’s fine if you are short, fat, flat, or skinny; it’s fine if you are ignorant. (Applause)

So God, through Reverend Moon, through the teacher, is trying to give everyone ideal love, ideal families, ideal tribes, ideal nations, ideal worlds, ideal universes, and even ideal love from God. God wants to make Himself the master of your home. If you think about it, it’s simple. Do you think you have received such things? Do you think you are receiving them? What is it? "I think I have received them."

Then, if you have received it, do you manage it? If you have received love, do you manage and use it? Therefore, I must create an environment where I can love. Just as God created what He could love, I must create what I can love. I must create a counterpart world. I must build a family that loves, a loving clan, a loving nation, a loving world, a loving heaven, and a loving God. And then I must manage it all with love. Isn’t that right? God created with love, manages with love, and does so to love again…. Don’t you want to be such a person? "I do." Is that easy? Is it easy? "No." Is it easier than going to Harvard and getting a Ph.D.? "It’s hard." How difficult would it be? The teacher has been doing this for 60 years, dedicating his whole life to this endeavor. There are no other thoughts. Do you want to inherit it? "Yes." The teacher is smart and naturally gifted, but I believe you are not as naturally gifted as the teacher and you are not as smart. (Laughter)

So, if the teacher has struggled this much, how much more must you struggle? How many times more must you struggle? So, when will you do it? Are you going to live for hundreds of years? Time is limited, and the tasks are immense, so you cannot afford to be slow. Is a teacher who teaches you to work harder than me a normal teacher, or is a teacher who says you can do less than me a normal teacher? "A teacher who teaches to work harder…" Those who have ears and thoughts should listen and act! So, do you want to try it? "Yes."

What we can boast about is that we have the ideal of the son-in-law. Now, what do you boast about? What do you have? What do you have? You have the ideal of the son-in-law. Then, do you want to just keep what you have in a warehouse? "No." You must create culture here, culture. Women also have the right to choose, and centered around this ideal, they must all act as artists, showcasing the love they possess.

If you have nothing, you must clench your fists and serve with a healthy body. You must do something, anything. Do not rely on the church, do not rely on the nation, do not rely on the world, do not rely on your parents, do not rely on God; be someone who creates reliance. If you decide to live your whole life for that, everything will become yours. Thus, in the family, you must not be a burden to your parents, and you must not rely on them. You must give for your siblings. You must serve society. In any era, the graves of those who died in debt… The indebted look at the ground, and those who have imposed debts look to the sky.

Reverend Moon understood this. I am not someone who came to America to be indebted to America. Everyone comes looking to be indebted to America, but I came to impose debts. It’s different. Many young people have flocked to America, but I am not someone who is indebted to you. I am imposing debts on you. I do not rely on my mother when I enter my home. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." If you have received a lot, you must give even more.

You are the same. In the future, who is high and who is not, do not think about that. Do not think about being recognized. This law is a law, and wherever you go… It’s fine if the teacher does not recognize you. According to this law, when it is against the law, it is always handled according to the standard of that law. You cannot complain about where you are going. Since I have not been responsible towards God, the nation, and the world, I must take responsibility and complain.

Now, you understand. So, do you want to go, have you got it? "I have." I have nothing. Reverend Moon has nothing. He has nothing. Young people of all colors follow Reverend Moon…. Those who come here to drink water will surely know the taste. Everyone should come here.

Look. Why does the spirit world cooperate with Reverend Moon? Why do they cooperate? There are many great people like established church pastors, Billy Graham, etc., but why does the spirit world cooperate centered on Reverend Moon? You must understand that clearly. If you understand it clearly and draw a conclusion, the spirit world must move according to that conclusion.

Today is June 10, 1979. Today, you have received something like this clearly. If you know for sure that the teacher has given this, and if you are convinced, you must go out with the feeling of "It is mine!" And if you have received it, you must give it. You must create a nation. Do you understand what I mean?

That nation is the nation of the father, the nation of God, the nation of the True Parents. Do you understand? I am sure that from now on, I see that I have it. When asked, "What do you have?" it was vague until now, but from now on, I truly have this ideal of love. Thank you! (Applause) 
*
